 in maukon par gaaya jaataa he jan-gana-man1
 When the nation gives the salute (it means the National Anthem - Salute Arms along with the National Anthem is presented to the President or the Governor / Lieutenant Governor inside the respective States / Union Territories on special occasions)
 2
 During the parade
 3
 On the arrival of the President in formal state functions and other events organized by the government and in mass programs and on his return from these programs
 4
 Before and after the President's address to the nation on All India Radio
 5
 On arrival of Governor / Lieutenant Governor in formal state programs within his / her State / Union Territory and at the time of their return from these programs
 6
 When the national flag is brought into the parade
 7
 When the colors of the regiment are presented
 8
 To hoist navy colors
